gacchōhanti guṇadharā, abābāhaṁ sivaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

ēva maṇiō surindō, añcanta harisiō puṇō namiuṁ

pucchaï kahēhi bhayava!, saṁpaï bhāmaṇḍalassa gaī

tō bhaṇaï sīradhārī, suravara! nimuṇēhi tāva saṁbandha

cariēṇa tujjha bhāyā, jēṇaṁ ciya pāviyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

aha kōsalāpurīē, ghaṇavantō asthi vajakō nāma

puttā asōya-tilyā, tassa piyā mayariyā bhajjā

nivāsiya suṇē, sōya sō duksimō taō jāō

cintēi sā araṇṇē, kaha kuṇaï thiī mahāpōrē:

ahiyē kivāluō sō, saṁviggō juimuṇissa sōsattaṁ

paḍivajiūṇa jāō samaṇō parivajjiyārambhō

aha annayā kayāī, asōga-tilayā gayā juimuṇindaṁ

paṇamanti āyarēṇaṁ, piyaraṁ ca puṇō puṇō tuṭṭhā

sōmaṇa dhammarayaṇaṁ, sahasā tē tibajāyasaṁvēgā

'dōṇi vi juissa pāsē, asōya-tilayā viṇikkhantā

kāaṇa tavaṁ ghōraṁ, kālāmō uvarimammi gēvējē

uvavannō tattha juī, mahājuī uttamō dēvō

tē tatya piyā putā, kukkuḍanayara samujjayā gantuṁ

saṁvēyajaṇiyabhāvā, vandaṇahēuṁ niṇindassa

pannāsa jōyaṇāī, gayāṇa aha annayā samaṇupattō

navapāusō mahāṣaṇataḍicchaḍāḍōvasalilōhō

tō girivarassa hēḍhē, jōgatthā muṇivarā dadadhiīyā

jantēṇa kōsalāē, dihā jaṇayassa puttēṇaṁ

cintēi imē sāhū, ihaṭṭhiyā samayarakkhaṇaṭṭāē

ghōrē upāsaṇaē, raṇē bahusāvayāiṇṇē

bhāmaṇḍalēṇa ēvaṁ, cintēuṁ pāṇarakkhaṇanimitaṁ

sāhūṇa samāsanē, vijāsu kayē puraṁ paramaṁ

kālē dēsē ya puraṁ, samāgayā gōcarēṇa tē samaṇā

paḍilāmēi mahappā, caṁuvihaāhāradāṇēṇaṁ

ēvaṁ kamēṇa tāṇaṁ, cāummāsī gayā muṇivarāṇaṁ

bhāmaṇḍalēṇa vi taō, dāṇaphalaṁ ajiya viulaṁ

bhāmaṇḍalō kayāī, saha sundaramahiliyāe ujjāṇē

asaṇihabhō ubavanō, dēvakurāē tipaścāū

dāṇēṇa bhōgabhūmī, lahaï narō tavaguṇēṇa dēvattaṁ

nāṇēṇaṁ siddhisuha, pāvaï nastva saṁdēhō

puṇaravi bhaṇaha surindō, ahōgaī lakkhaṇō samaṇupattō

ubaṭṭō ya mahāmaṇi!, ṭhāṇaṁ kavaṇaṁ tu pāvihiha

nijariya kammanibaha, labhihī kavaṇaṁ gaī ca dahavayaṇō:

kō va bhavōhāmi ahaṁ!, ēvaṁ icchāmi nāu jē

bhaṇaï taō baladēvō, suṇēhi dēvinda! āgamissāṇaṁ

uktiṇaṁ bhavāṇaṁ, lahāhiva-lacchinilayāṇaṁ

narayāu samuttiṇṇā, kamēṇa surapavayassa puṣēṇaṁ

vijayāvahanayarīē, maṇuyā tē dō vi hōhinti

tāṇaṁ piyā suṇandō, jaṇaṇī vi ya havaha rōhiṇī nāma

sāvayakulasaṁbhūyā, gurudēvayapūyaṇāhirayā

aïsundarasvadharā, nāmēṇaṁ arahadāsa-siridāsā

kāūṇa sāvayattaṁ, dēvā hōhinti suralōē

cajhyā tatyēva purē, maṇuyā hōūṇa sāvayā paramā

muṇivaradāṇaphalēṇaṁ, hōhinti narā ya harivarisē

bhōga bhōttūṇa mayā, dēvā hōhinti dēvalōgammi

caïyā tatthēva purē, naravaïputtā havīhanti

vāukumārassa suyā, lacchīdēvīe kucchisaṁbhūyā

amarindasarisarūvā, jayakanta-jayappahā dhōrā

kāūṇa tavamuyāra, dēvā hōhinti lantaē kappē

uttamabhōgaṭhiīyā, uttamaguṇadhārayā dhīrā

tuhamavi iha bharahē khala, caūṇaṁ añcuyāu kappāō

cōisarayaṇāhivāī, cakkaharō hōhisi nirutaṁ

tē cēva surā caïyā, dōṇi vi tuha nandaṇā bhavīhanti

induraha-bhōyarahā, amarakumārōvamasirīyā

paranārivajaṇēṇaṁ, vaēṇa ēkēṇa sō hu dahavayaṇō

jāō ciya indurahō, sammataparāyaṇō dhīrō

sō cēva ya indurahō, labhiūṇa bhavā imā surāīyā

pacchā hōhaï arahā, samatthatēlōkaparimahiō

aha sō vi cakvaṭṭī, rajja rayaṇatyalē purē kāuṁ

hōhaï tavōbalēṇaṁ, ahamindō vējayantammi

sō hu tuma samgāō, caïō arahassa tassa gaṇapavarō

hōmaga tihuyaṇamga, siddhisuhaṁ cēva pāvihisi

ēsō tē parikahiō, dasāṇaṇō saha tumē surāhivaī!

ēttō suṇāhi puṇaravi, lakkhaṇapagayaṁ bhaṇijjantaṁ

jō sō'yaṁ bhōyarahō, cakkaharasuō tavaṣpabhāvaṇaṁ

bhamiūṇa uttamabhavē, kēī daḍhadhammasaṁjuttō

pukkharadīvavidēhē, paümapurē lakṣaṇō u cakkaharō

hōhii titthayarō puṇa, tatyēva bhavē tiyasaṇāhō

satsu varisēsu jiṇō, kāūṇa asēsadōsasaṁghāraṁ

sura-asuranamiyacalaṇō, pāvihii aṇuttaraṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

ēvaṁ kēvalikahiyaṁ, bhavissabhavasaṁkahaṁ suṇēūṇaṁ

jāō saṁsayarahiō, paḍiindō bhāvaṇājuttō

namiūṇa rāmadēvaṁ, tāhē sabāyarēṇa puṇarutaṁ

abhivandaï surapavarō, niṇavarabhavaṇāī vivihāī

nandīsarāiyāī, abhivandēūṇa cēiyaharāī

kuruvaṁ ciya saṁpattō, pēcchada bhāmaṇḍalaṁ dēvō

saṁbhāsiūṇa payaō, saṁbōhiya bhāyaraṁ siṇēhēṇaṁ

vibuhāhivō khaṇēṇaṁ, saṁpattō accurya kappaṁ

tatyāraṇapuē sō, amaravalsayasahassaparikiṇṇō

aṇuhavaï uttamasuha, sīindō sumahayaṁ kālaṁ

pannarasa sahassāī, barisāṇa tayā''si āuya haliṇō

sōlasa cāvāṇi puṇō, uccattaṁ cēva nāyavaṁ

pēcchaha balēṇa mahayā, niṇindavarasāsaṇē ghiī kārḍa

jamma-jarā-maraṇarivū, parājiyā ghīrasattaṇaṁ

nissēsadōsarahimaō, nāṇāaïsayavibhūsaṁjuttō

kēvalakiraṇujaliō, vibhāi saraē va divasayarō

ārāhiūṇa dhīrō, jiṇasamayaṁ pañcavīsa varisāī

āukkhayammi pattō, paümō sivasāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ

vigayabhavahēugaṁ taṁ, aṇagāraṁ suddhasīlasammattaṁ

sabāyarēṇa paṇamaha, dukkhakkhayakārayaṁ rāmaṁ

pubasiṇēhēṇa tayā, sīyādēvāhivēṇa parimahiyaṁ

paramiḍḍisaṁpaüttaṁ, paṇamaha rāma maṇōrāmaṁ

ikkhāgavaṁsatilayaṁ, iha bharahē aṭṭamaṁ tu baladēvaṁ

taṁ namaha ṇēyabhavasayasahassamukkaṁ sivapayatthaṁ

ēyaṁ halaharacariyaṁ, niyayaṁ jō suṇaï suddhabhāvaṇaṁ

sō lahaï bōhilābha, buddhi-balā''uṁca aïparamaṁ

ujjayasatyō vi rikhū, khippaṁ uvasamaï tassa uvasamgō

ajiṇaī cēva puṇṇaṁ, nasēṇa samayaṁ na saṁdēhō

rajjarahiō vi rajaṁ, lahaï dhaṇatthī mahādhaṇaṁ viulaṁ

uvasamaï takkhaṇaṁ ciya, vāhī sōmā ya hōnti gahā

mahilatthī varamahilaṁ, puttatthī gōttanandaṇaṁ puttaṁ

lahaï paradēsagamaṇē, samāgamaṁ cēva bandhūṇaṁ

dubbhāsiyāī duñcintiyāī duścariyasayasahassāī

nāsanti paümakittaṇakahāe dūra samatthāī

naṁ pi ya jaṇassa hiyaēṁ, avaṭṭiyaṁ kāraṇaṁ aïmahantaṁ

taṁ tassa nicchaēṇaṁ, uvaṇamaï suhāṇubandhēṇaṁ

ēvaṁ dhammōvāyā, siṭṭhā tava-niyama-sīlamāīyā

titthayarēhi mahānasa!, aṇantanāṇuttamadharēhiṁ

niyayaṁ karēha bhatti, jiṇāṇa maṇa-vayaṇa-kāyasaṁjuttā

jēṇa'ṭṭakammarahiyā, pāvaha siddhiṁ suvīsatthā

ēvaṁ visuddhalaliyakkharahēujutaṁ, askhāṇaēmu vivihēsu nibaddhamatthaṁ

nāsēi duggaïpaha" khalu nicchaēṇaṁ, rāmāravindacariyaṁ tu suyaṁ samatthaṁ

ēvaṁ vīrajiṇēṇa rāmacariya siṭuṁ mahatthaṁ purā, pacchā''khaṇḍalabhūiṇā u kahiyaṁ sīsāṇa dhammāsayaṁ

bhūō sāhuparaṁparāe, sayalaṁ lōē ṭhiyaṁ pāyarḍa, ēttāhē vimalēṇa suttasahiyaṁ gāhānibaddha kayaṁ

pañcēva ya bāsasayā, dusamāē tīsavarisasaṁjulā

vīrē siddhimuvagaē, taō nibaddha imaṁ cariyaṁ

halahara-cakaharāṇaṁ, samaya lavāhivēṇa jaṁ vatta

visayāmisasattāṇa, ithinimittaṁ raṇaṁ paramaṁ

bahujuvaïsahassēhiṁ, na ya pattō uvasamaṁ mayaṇamūḍhō

sō vijāhararāyā, gaō ya naraya aṇimiyappā

jō'ṇēyapaṇaïṇīhiṁ, lālijjantō vi na ya gaō tittiṁ

kaha puṇa annō tuṣṭuiṁ, vañcihii suthōvavilayāhiṁ?

jē visayasuhāsattā, purisā taba-niyama-saṁjamavihūṇā

tē ujjhiūṇa rayaṇaṁ, gēhanti hu kāgiṇiṁ mūḍhā

ēvaṁ vēranimitta, paranārīsaṁsiya suṇēūṇaṁ

hōha paralōyakalī, paravilayaṁ cēva bajēha

sukayaphalēṇa maṇussō, pāvaï ṭhāṇaṁ susaṁpayanihāṇaṁ

dukayaphalēṇa ya kugaī, lahaï sahāvō imō lōē

na ya dēi kōi kassaï, ārōggadhaṇaṁ tahēva paramāuṁ

naï dēnti surā lōē, taha vi hu kiṁ dukkhiyā bahavē?

kāma-stha-dhamma-mōkkhā, ēttha purāṇammi vaṇṇiyā sabaï

aguṇē mōttūṇa guṇē, gēṇhaha jē tumha hiyajaṇaṇē

bahuēṇa kiṁ va kīraï, abō bhaṇiyabaēṇa lōyammi?

ēkkaṣayammi vi bujhaha, ramaha sayā niṇavaramayammi

viṇasāsaṇāṇuraṇa, hōūṇaṁ kumaha uttama dharma

jēṇa avigdhaṁ pāvaha, baladēvāī gayā natya

ēmaṁ rāhacariyaṁ, sabā vi ya samayadēvayā niyayaṁ

kuāntu saṁsaṇijja, jaṇaṁ ca niyamattisaṁjutaṁ

svatantu bhaviyalōya, sūrāīyā gahā aparisēsā

susamāhiyasōmamaṇā, jiṇavaradhammujjayamaīyā

aṇaṁ ahari bā, jē ēstha kayaṁ pamāyadōsēṇaṁ

taṁ mē paḍipūrē, khamantu iha paṇḍiyā saī

rāhū nāmāyariō, sasamayaparasamayagahiyasabbhāvō

'vijaō ya tassa sīsō, nāilakulavaṁsanandiyarō

sīsēṇa tassa raïyaṁ, rāhavacariyaṁ tu sūrivimalēṇaṁ

sōūṇaṁ puṣagaē, nārāyaṇaṁ-sīricariyāī

jēhiṁ surya vavagayamaccharēhiṁ tabbhatibhāviyamaṇēhiṁ

tāṇaṁ vihēu bōhiṁ, bimalaṁ cariya supurisāṇaṁ
